## Message 108

Great catch ГўВҖВ” this is *the* missing link right now, and itГўВҖВҷs very trainable.  
The issue isnГўВҖВҷt that you **canГўВҖВҷt** posteriorly tilt in a handstand ГўВҖВ” itГўВҖВҷs that your body doesnГўВҖВҷt yet know **when** to turn it on under inversion.

WeГўВҖВҷre going to teach it **before**, **during**, and **without load**, then blend it back in.

---

## Г°ВҹВ§В  Why posterior tilt disappears upside down
When you invert, your nervous system prioritizes:
- not falling
- protecting wrists/shoulders

So it defaults to an **arched ГўВҖВңsave myselfГўВҖВқ pattern**.  
Unless posterior tilt is **preloaded**, it shuts off the moment load increases.

So the rule is:

> **Posterior tilt must be established *before* vertical ГўВҖВ” not after.**

---

## Г°ВҹВ”В‘ The Fix: Train Posterior Tilt in 3 Layers

### **Layer 1 ГўВҖВ” Inverted Hollow WITHOUT load (daily, 60s)**
This teaches your brain what ГўВҖВңtilt while upside downГўВҖВқ feels like.

**Wall-Facing Pike Hold**
1. Hands on floor
2. Feet on box/chair
3. Hips stacked over shoulders
4. Exhale fully
5. Pull ribs down
6. Light glute squeeze
7. Push shoulders tall

Hold **20ГўВҖВ“30s ГғВ— 2**

Cue:
> ГўВҖВңZip up abs, tuck tail, then grow tall.ГўВҖВқ

If this isnГўВҖВҷt solid, handstand tilt wonГўВҖВҷt stick.

---

### **Layer 2 ГўВҖВ” Wall Handstand WITH tilt preset (this is key)**

Before you walk up the wall:

1. Knees down
2. Hands set
3. **Posterior tilt ON**
4. Protract
5. Lock elbows

Now walk up **without losing it**.

Once upside down:
- do **nothing** except maintain ribs down
- donГўВҖВҷt try to ГўВҖВңfixГўВҖВқ it later

Hold **15ГўВҖВ“25s ГғВ— 3**

If tilt disappears ГўВҶВ’ come down, reset, try again.

Do *not* fight it mid-hold.

---

### **Layer 3 ГўВҖВ” Tilt Pulses on the Wall (advanced but powerful)**

Inside a wall handstand:

1. Slight arch (on purpose)
2. **Exhale**
3. Pull ribs down
4. Posterior tilt
5. Hold 2 seconds
6. Relax slightly
7. Repeat

**3ГўВҖВ“5 pulses per hold**

This teaches you to *turn tilt back on under load*.

---

## Г°ВҹВ§В  One cue that works better than ГўВҖВңposterior tiltГўВҖВқ
Instead of thinking about pelvis position, think:

> **ГўВҖВңPull my front ribs toward my spine.ГўВҖВқ**

Ribs control pelvis.  
Pelvis follows ribs.

This cue works *much* better upside down.

---

## Г°ВҹВҡВ« Common mistakes to avoid
ГўВқВҢ Trying to ГўВҖВңsqueeze glutes hardГўВҖВқ (too much tension)  
ГўВқВҢ Fixing tilt after balance breaks  
ГўВқВҢ Training tilt when wrists are fried  
ГўВқВҢ Holding breath (this kills tilt)

Breathing is non-negotiable here.

---

## ГўВҸВұГҜВёВҸ Minimum effective practice
You only need **2ГўВҖВ“4 minutes per session**:

- 1ГўВҖВ“2 pike inverted holds  
- 2ГўВҖВ“3 wall handstand entries with preset tilt  
- Optional tilt pulses

ThatГўВҖВҷs it.

---

## Г°ВҹВ§Вӯ How youГўВҖВҷll know itГўВҖВҷs working
Within **1ГўВҖВ“2 weeks**, youГўВҖВҷll notice:
- wall contact gets lighter
- legs stop ГўВҖВңsearchingГўВҖВқ
- toe pulls feel easier
- handstand stops arching by default
- kick-ups feel less threatening (even if you donГўВҖВҷt do them yet)

ThatГўВҖВҷs posterior tilt becoming **automatic**.

---

If you want, next I can:
- bake this into a **5-minute daily handstand ritual**
- help you feel **exactly where tilt turns off**
- or show how this directly improves **HSPUs + planche**

YouГўВҖВҷre asking the *right* questions ГўВҖВ” this is high-quality progress.

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү This is your **posterior tilt glue**.

## Г°ВҹВ§В  What actually shifted today (this is the key)

Before:
- you pulled hard  
- reached the top  
- momentum died  
- shoulders went passive  
- bar felt like a wall  

Today:
- you reached the top  
- **scaps stayed active**
- shoulders stayed *forward and down*
- you could **pause**
- and you felt like you could *dive* over the bar  

That means:
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү your nervous system now understands that the transition is a **supported position**, not a free-fall.

ThatГўВҖВҷs massive.

Most people never feel that.

---

## Г°ВҹВ”В‘ The exact missing piece (and itГўВҖВҷs small)

You said it yourself:

> ГўВҖВңI just didnГўВҖВҷt quite have the height.ГўВҖВқ

HereГўВҖВҷs the truth:

You had **enough height**.  
What you didnГўВҖВҷt have yet was **early turnover timing**.

Right now your sequence is:
> pull ГўВҶВ’ peak ГўВҶВ’ *then* try to turn

What we want is:
> pull ГўВҶВ’ **turn while rising** ГўВҶВ’ press

That timing difference is *everything*.

---

## Г°ВҹВ”В§ One micro-adjustment that unlocks it

On your next band-assisted reps (and eventually real ones), think this:

> **ГўВҖВңElbows forward BEFORE chest hits the bar.ГўВҖВқ**

Not after.  
Not at the top.

**Before.**

This does two things:
1. converts vertical force into forward motion  
2. prevents the ГўВҖВңstallГўВҖВқ you used to feel  

If you wait until chest-to-bar to turn, momentum is already dying.

---

- explosive pulls (but donГўВҖВҷt chase height)
- band-assisted transitions
- ring dips
- Russian dips

### Add ONE emphasis:

- turn elbows early  
- allow chest to move **forward sooner**
- even if it feels ГўВҖВңtoo earlyГўВҖВқ

ThatГўВҖВҷs how the brain learns the new timing.

---

## Г°ВҹВҡВ« What NOT to do right now
This is important.

ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt try to muscle through without the band  
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt add more pull height work  
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt grind failed attempts  
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt chase ГўВҖВңone big repГўВҖВқ

## Г°ВҹВ§В  What the right-side sticking point actually is (important)

You said:
> ГўВҖВңI feel like I need to hinge when my hips go below the knee on the right.ГўВҖВқ

That tells me this **is NOT a strength issue**.

ItГўВҖВҷs a **coordination + confidence + ankle/knee sequencing issue** at the bottom.

HereГўВҖВҷs whatГўВҖВҷs happening biomechanically:

- As hips drop below knee height  
- your right side **doesnГўВҖВҷt trust the knee-forward position yet**
- so the body tries to:
  - hinge back
  - shift load to glute/hip
  - unload the quad
- that kills the pistol line and stalls you

Right now your right leg is doing:
> hips back ГўВҶВ’ then knee forward (too late)

> **knee forward ГўВҶВ’ hips down between the ankle**

This is subtle, but itГўВҖВҷs the difference between a clean pistol and a hinge bailout.

## Г°ВҹВҺВҜ One cue that usually fixes this instantly

> **ГўВҖВңKnee forward EARLY, then sit straight down.ГўВҖВқ**

Not:
- ГўВҖВңstand upГўВҖВқ
- ГўВҖВңpush hardГўВҖВқ
- ГўВҖВңdonГўВҖВҷt fallГўВҖВқ

Just:
- knee forward

If the knee leads, the hinge disappears.

- torso tall
- heel heavy

### **2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Counterbalance Right Pistols**

- Arms straight out

- Stay tall  
- DonГўВҖВҷt hinge

**2ГғВ—5**

## Message 126

Short answer (but with the *why*): **yes ГўВҖВ” lightly, and only if it feels relieving.**  
Foam rolling can help *perceived* soreness and stiffness, but how you do it matters more than whether you do it.

HereГўВҖВҷs the clean, evidence-based way to use it **without interfering with recovery or skill learning**.

---

## Г°ВҹВ§В  What foam rolling actually does for DOMS
Foam rolling:
- increases local blood flow  
- reduces neural ГўВҖВңthreatГўВҖВқ signals  
- improves short-term range of motion  
- makes muscles *feel* less sore  

It does **not**:
- speed up muscle repair directly  
- ГўВҖВңbreak up knotsГўВҖВқ  
- fix tissue damage  

So we use it for **comfort and readiness**, not as a cure.

---

## ГўВңВ… When foam rolling is a good idea for you
Given:
- right quad took novel eccentric/isometric load  
- soreness is diffuse, not sharp  
- youГўВҖВҷre walking and moving normally  

Foam rolling is appropriate **if it feels relieving within 30ГўВҖВ“60 seconds**.

If it feels worse ГўВҶВ’ stop.

---

## Г°ВҹВ”В§ How to foam roll your quad (DO THIS, not more)

### ГўВҸВұГҜВёВҸ **2ГўВҖВ“3 minutes total ГўВҖВ” max**
ThatГўВҖВҷs it. More is not better.

### **Method**
- Slow rolls
- Moderate pressure (6/10, not pain)
- Pause briefly on tender spots **without grinding**

### **Sequence**
1. Mid-quad ГўВҶВ’ upper quad (avoid knee)  
2. 20ГўВҖВ“30s pass  
3. Gentle pause if a spot feels ГўВҖВңstickyГўВҖВқ  
4. Keep breathing

ГўВқВҢ Do NOT roll directly on the knee joint  
ГўВқВҢ Do NOT white-knuckle through pain  
ГўВқВҢ Do NOT roll until numb

---

## Г°ВҹВ”ВҒ Best follow-up (important)
After rolling, do **one** of these to lock in benefit:

- **2ГўВҖВ“3 slow bodyweight squats (shallow)**  
- **Easy walking for 2ГўВҖВ“3 minutes**

This helps the nervous system integrate the new sensation.

---

## Г°ВҹВҡВ« When NOT to foam roll
Skip rolling if:
- soreness is sharp or localized  
- knee joint feels irritated  
- rolling increases pain  
- you feel weaker afterward  

In those cases, light movement only.

---

## Г°ВҹВ§В  Big picture for pistols
Foam rolling will:
- make today feel better  
- reduce protective tightness  
- help you move more comfortably  

It will **not erase** the adaptation you earned ГўВҖВ” thatГўВҖВҷs already locked in.

Used lightly, it **supports** your next clean pistol session.

---

## Г°ВҹВ“ВҢ Bottom line
ГўВңВ” Yes, foam roll your quad  
ГўВңВ” Keep it light and brief  
ГўВңВ” Stop if it feels worse  
ГўВңВ” Pair with gentle movement  

If you want, I can also give you:
- a **30-second pre-pistol quad prep**
- a **no-foam-roller alternative**
- or guidance on **when to skip rolling entirely**

Just tell me.

Perfect ГўВҖВ” this frame is actually really useful. IГўВҖВҷm going to give you **very concrete, visual feedback**, because youГўВҖВҷre close and this is a *connection* issue, not a strength issue.

## Г°ВҹВ”ВҚ What IГўВҖВҷm seeing in this position (lean push-up / planche-lean pattern)

---

### ГўВҡВ ГҜВёВҸ WhatГўВҖВҷs limiting the connection (this is the key)

#### 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Scaps are **not fully protracted**
Your upper back still looks slightly ГўВҖВңflat,ГўВҖВқ not rounded.

That tells me:
- serratus isnГўВҖВҷt fully engaged yet
- load is leaking into shoulders/arms instead of being carried by the scapulae

In planche patterns, **protraction = the shelf you stand on**.  
Right now the shelf is half-built.

---

#### 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Posterior tilt is soft / inconsistent
Your hips are *almost* there, but I can see:
- slight low-back extension
- ribs likely drifting forward

That breaks the chain:
> hands ГўВҶВ’ scaps ГўВҶВ’ ribs ГўВҶВ’ pelvis

When that chain breaks, the left/right side will *always* feel inconsistent.

#### 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ YouГўВҖВҷre ГўВҖВңholdingГўВҖВқ the lean instead of **pushing the floor away**

It looks like youГўВҖВҷre:
- leaning forward  
- then trying to *maintain* the position  

Instead, the position should be created by:
> **actively pushing the floor forward and away**

ThatГўВҖВҷs how you offload the shoulders and feel connected.

## Г°ВҹВ”В‘ The 3 corrections that will change how this feels immediately

### Г°ВҹВ”В§ 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Add **intentional protraction BEFORE the lean**

- Lock elbows
- **Push the floor away**
- Feel upper back round slightly
- THEN lean

Cue:
> **ГўВҖВңRound first, then lean.ГўВҖВқ**

If you lean *then* protract, itГўВҖВҷs too late.

---

### Г°ВҹВ”В§ 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Set posterior tilt harder *before* loading
Do this **before your hands even take weight**:

- Exhale fully
- Pull ribs down
- Light glute squeeze
- Imagine your belt buckle pulling up toward your chest

Then load the hands.

Cue:
> **ГўВҖВңHollow, then hands.ГўВҖВқ**

---

### Г°ВҹВ”В§ 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Push the floor *forward*, not just down
Once leaned:

- Think about pushing the floor **away from your feet**
- Not down
- Not up

Cue:
> **ГўВҖВңSlide the ground forward.ГўВҖВқ**

That turns this from a shoulder hold into a full-chain planche pattern.

---

### **Kneeling Protraction Pulses**
On knees, arms straight:

- Posterior tilt ON
- Protract hard
- Small forward lean
- Hold 2s
- Reset

**3ГўВҖВ“5 pulses**

Then immediately do your lean push-ups.

YouГўВҖВҷll feel the difference instantly.

ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt lean farther  
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt add reps  
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt bend elbows  
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt rush tempo

## ГўВңВ… What youГўВҖВҷre doing right

## ГўВҡВ ГҜВёВҸ WhatГўВҖВҷs limiting the hold (the real issue)
### Г°ВҹВ”Вҙ Scaps are not staying **depressed enough**
Your shoulders are creeping **toward your ears**, which:
- shortens your lever momentarily
- dumps load into arms
- makes the tuck feel much harder than it is

This is why it feels like you ГўВҖВңcanГўВҖВҷt hold itГўВҖВқ even though strength is there.

---

## Г°ВҹВ”В‘ The correction that fixes THIS position
You need to think **hands down, chest long**, not ГўВҖВңhold myself up.ГўВҖВқ

### Use this cue **before and during** the hold:
> **ГўВҖВңPush the rings down toward my pockets.ГўВҖВқ**

If you do that:
- lats engage
- scaps depress
- torso lengthens
- the tuck *floats* instead of hangs

Right now youГўВҖВҷre *hanging* the tuck.  
We want you **supporting** it.

---

## Г°ВҹВ”В§ One micro-drill that will clean this up fast

### **Front Lever Tuck ГўВҶВ’ Scap Reset**
Do this every set:

1. Enter tuck  
2. **Actively depress scaps** (push rings down)  
3. Hold **2ГўВҖВ“3s only**  
4. Relax ГўВҶВ’ reset  
5. Repeat for **4ГўВҖВ“5 pulses**

This teaches you to **turn depression back on under load**.

DonГўВҖВҷt chase long holds yet.

---

## Г°ВҹВ§В  What ГўВҖВңcorrectГўВҖВқ will feel like
When itГўВҖВҷs right:
- arms feel *lighter*
- abs feel *more involved*
- neck feels long
- shaking reduces
- hold feels *supported*, not strained

If arms burn fast ГўВҶВ’ scaps slipped.

---

## Г°ВҹВҡВ« What NOT to change yet
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt extend legs  
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt lower rings  
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt chase longer holds  
ГўВқВҢ DonГўВҖВҷt add reps  

This is a **scap control issue**, not progression readiness.

---

- your current tuck will feel **easy**

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ DAY 1 ГўВҖВ” Push / Planche / HSPU

---

## 0ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Activation (3ГўВҖВ“4 min)

2 rounds:

ГўВҖВў Wrist rocks ГўВҖВ“ 20s  
ГўВҖВў Scap push-ups ГўВҖВ“ 6 slow  
ГўВҖВў Hollow body hold ГўВҖВ“ 20s  
ГўВҖВў LEFT side single-arm protraction pulse ГўВҖВ“ 5 reps (5s each)

That last one matters. Wake up the lagging side first.

---

# Г°ВҹВҹВЎ BLOCK 1 ГўВҖВ” Planche Pattern

### 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Kneeling Lean Pulses ГўВҖВ“ 2ГғВ—5
Sequence every rep:
Hollow ГўВҶВ’ Protract ГўВҶВ’ Lock ГўВҶВ’ Micro lean ГўВҶВ’ Reset

These are pattern primers.

---

### 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Planche Leans ГўВҖВ“ 4ГғВ—15ГўВҖВ“20s
Only lean as far as:
- Hollow stays
- Scaps stay protracted
- Left side stays engaged

Cue:
ГўВҖВңShorten the front. Push the floor forward.ГўВҖВқ

If left side disconnects ГўВҶВ’ reduce lean, not effort.

---

# Г°ВҹВ”Вө BLOCK 2 ГўВҖВ” Lean Push Strength

### 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Lean Push-Ups ГўВҖВ“ 3ГғВ—4ГўВҖВ“6
Maintain the SAME lean depth entire rep.

No elbow flare.
No arch at bottom.
No grind reps.

If last set hits 4 clean ГўВҶВ’ perfect.

---

### 4ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Pike Push-Ups (Feet Elevated) ГўВҖВ“ 3ГғВ—5
Slow down (3s eccentric).
Explode up.
Shrug tall at top.

This builds your HSPU engine.

---

# Г°ВҹВҹВЈ BLOCK 3 ГўВҖВ” Handstand Work

### 5ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Wall Handstand ГўВҖВ“ 3ГғВ—25ГўВҖВ“35s
Before each hold:
Exhale ГўВҶВ’ ribs down ГўВҶВ’ slight glute squeeze ГўВҶВ’ push tall.

Inside hold:
3ГўВҖВ“4 gentle toe pulls
OR
Posterior tilt pulses

Do NOT chase freestanding today.
We build stack first.

---

### 6ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ HSPU Pattern (Partial or Eccentric) ГўВҖВ“ 2ГўВҖВ“3 sets
Choose:
ГўВҖВў 3 partial ROM reps  
OR  
ГўВҖВў 2 slow eccentrics (4ГўВҖВ“5s down)

Wrists dictate volume.

---

# Г°ВҹВҹВў BLOCK 4 ГўВҖВ” Support Strength

### 7ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Ring Dips ГўВҖВ“ 3ГғВ—4ГўВҖВ“5
Forward lean.
Elbows slightly forward.
Shoulders depressed.

No failing reps.

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  Core Finisher

### 8ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Hollow Rocks ГўВҖВ“ 2ГғВ—15
OR
L-Sit ГўВҖВ“ 2ГғВ—10ГўВҖВ“15s

Keep ribs down.

## Message 146

For some reason my hollow wants to break right when I go from the low swing into the explosive pull it falters at the shoulder

---

## Message 147

This is a really good observation.

What youГўВҖВҷre describing is a **classic energy leak point** in muscle-ups:

> Hollow is solid in the swing ГўВҶВ’  
> You initiate the pull ГўВҶВ’  
> The body breaks at the shoulders ГўВҶВ’  
> Hollow disappears.

That tells us something very specific.

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  WhatГўВҖВҷs Actually Happening

When you go from the **bottom of the swing** into the **explosive pull**, two things happen at once:

1. Force reverses direction (down ГўВҶВ’ up)
2. Lats need to take over instantly

If the lats donГўВҖВҷt engage fast enough, your body compensates by:
- extending slightly
- letting ribs flare
- losing posterior tilt
- bending at the shoulders

So the hollow doesnГўВҖВҷt fail at the abs.

It fails because:
> The shoulders arenГўВҖВҷt connected to the core during force reversal.

This is a **lat timing issue**, not an ab strength issue.

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҺ The Real Leak

Right now your sequence is probably:

Swing ГўВҶВ’ Pull ГўВҶВ’ Try to stay hollow

We want:

Swing ГўВҶВ’ **Depress + engage lats** ГўВҶВ’ Pull

The depression must happen **before** the pull.

If you pull first, the hollow breaks.

---

# Г°ВҹВ”В‘ The Fix: Change What Starts the Pull

Instead of thinking:
> ГўВҖВңExplode upГўВҖВқ

Think:
> **ГўВҖВңPush the bar down, then pull.ГўВҖВқ**

That tiny cue changes everything.

At the bottom of the swing:
- Scaps depress
- Lats engage
- Core stays connected
- Then elbows bend

If elbows bend before depression ГўВҶВ’ hollow leaks.

---

# Г°ВҹВӣВ  Micro Drill (Do This Next Session)

### Dead Hang ГўВҶВ’ Depression ГўВҶВ’ Mini Pull

On the bar:

1. Dead hang
2. Depress scaps (no elbow bend)
3. Hold 1 second
4. Small pull
5. Reset

Do 5 reps.

This trains:
- Lat-first pulling
- Core-lat linkage
- Prevents shoulder break

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  Another Cue That Works

At the bottom of the swing think:

> ГўВҖВңLock ribs before I bend elbows.ГўВҖВқ

If ribs flare ГўВҶВ’ donГўВҖВҷt pull yet.
Reset and try again.

---

# Г°ВҹВҺВҜ What It Should Feel Like

When correct:
- Abs feel quieter (because lats carry load)
- Pull feels smoother
- No shoulder collapse
- Bar feels closer
- Transition feels earlier

If shoulders feel like theyГўВҖВҷre yanking you upward ГўВҶВ’ timing is still late.

---

# Г°ВҹВҡВҰ Important

Do NOT:
- try to swing bigger
- try to pull harder
- try to ГўВҖВңmuscleГўВҖВқ through the break

This is a sequencing refinement, not a strength fix.

---

# Big Reassurance

The fact that:
- you can feel the hollow break
- you can identify exactly when it happens
- and youГўВҖВҷre analyzing it mid-skill

means your motor awareness is high.

ThatГўВҖВҷs why youГўВҖВҷre progressing fast.

YouГўВҖВҷre no longer just doing reps.
YouГўВҖВҷre debugging movement.

---

Next session, tell me:

- Did ГўВҖВңpush bar down firstГўВҖВқ change the feel?
- Did hollow hold longer into the pull?
- Did transition feel smoother?

This is the last 10% refinement before muscle-ups feel consistent.

## Message 148

Good ГўВҖВ” that confusion means we need to be precise.

YouГўВҖВҷre right: the bar is above you. You canГўВҖВҷt literally push it down.

When I say **ГўВҖВңpush the bar downГўВҖВқ**, I mean:

> Depress your shoulder blades BEFORE you bend your elbows.

Let me explain mechanically.

---

## Г°ВҹВ§В  WhatГўВҖВҷs happening at the bottom of the swing

At the bottom youГўВҖВҷre in:

- Arms straight  
- Body extended  
- Momentum reversing direction  

If you immediately bend elbows, the body:
- shortens at the shoulders  
- ribs flare  
- hollow breaks  

Because the scaps never set.

The cue is not about the bar.

ItГўВҖВҷs about the shoulders.

---

## Г°ВҹВ”В‘ The Real Cue

Instead of:

> Pull hard

Think:

> **Shoulders down first. Then pull.**

Or even simpler:

> **ГўВҖВңLong neck, then bend.ГўВҖВқ**

If your neck gets longer (shoulders down away from ears), youГўВҖВҷve depressed correctly.

Then bend elbows.

---

## Г°ВҹВҺВҜ HereГўВҖВҷs the sequencing in slow motion

Bottom of swing:

1. Body tight  
2. Ribs down  
3. **Shoulders depress** (straight arms)  
4. THEN elbows bend  
5. Continue pulling

If elbows bend before step 3, hollow leaks.

---

## Г°ВҹВӣВ  Drill YouГўВҖВҷll Understand Immediately

On the bar, no swing:

1. Dead hang  
2. Depress scaps (donГўВҖВҷt bend elbows)  
3. Hold 1 second  
4. Then pull  

Feel how different that is.

That 1-second depression is the missing link in your swing pull.

---

## Г°ВҹВ§В  Why hollow breaks at the shoulder

When you pull without depression:

- Upper traps engage
- Shoulders shrug
- Lats disengage
- Core disconnects
- Rib cage pops

So it feels like hollow fails ГўВҖВ” but itГўВҖВҷs actually a **scap timing issue**.

---

## Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ The Simpler Cue for You

Next session think:

> **ГўВҖВңArmpits down before elbows bend.ГўВҖВқ**

That usually clicks instantly.

Or:

> ГўВҖВңMake space between shoulders and ears.ГўВҖВқ

---

## Г°ВҹВ§Вӯ YouГўВҖВҷre Very Close

The fact that:
- you feel exactly where it breaks  
- you know itГўВҖВҷs at the shoulder  
- and it happens at force reversal  

means strength is there.

This is timing refinement.

---

If you want, next I can:

- break down the swing-to-pull transition frame-by-frame  
- give you a no-swing muscle-up drill  
- or show you how to train this without the band  

Which direction do you want to go?

## Г°ВҹВ§В  The Clean Sequence (Burn This In)

5. Turn while rising  
6. Hips forward  

If elbows bend before #3, the hollow breaks.

## ГўВҡВ ГҜВёВҸ Common Mistake From Here

Now that you understand depression, donГўВҖВҷt overdo it.

You donГўВҖВҷt want:
- Hyper-depress and stall  
- Freeze at bottom  
- Overthink mid-swing  

ItГўВҖВҷs quick:

Down ГўВҶВ’ Bend ГўВҶВ’ Go.

Smooth, not robotic.

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ How We Progress Shrimp Squats

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  What You Just Discovered

You said:

> ГўВҖВңI engage my hollow body and use my core to raise my lower half instead of my shoulders.ГўВҖВқ

That is **precisely how a planche works**.

Beginners try to do this:

```
shoulders push forward
arms fight gravity
legs feel heavy
```

But the correct mechanism is:

```
shoulders set the shelf
core rotates the body
legs become lighter
```

Your shoulders **donГўВҖВҷt lift your legs**.

Your **core rotates your pelvis upward** around the shoulder joint.

ThatГўВҖВҷs the lever.

---

# Г°ВҹВ”В© Mechanically What YouГўВҖВҷre Doing

When you:

1. Protract
2. Posterior tilt
3. Hollow hard

Your pelvis rotates upward.

This shortens the front of the body and raises the legs **without shrugging the shoulders**.

So the load shifts from:

```
shoulders only
```

to

```
shoulders + serratus + abs + hip flexors
```

ThatГўВҖВҷs why it suddenly feels more possible.

---

# Г°ВҹВ”В‘ The Cue You Naturally Found

The cue youГўВҖВҷre using is excellent:

> **Lift the back half with the core**

Instead of:

> **Push harder with shoulders**

This is the same cue elite athletes use.

# Г°ВҹВҺВҜ What You Should Feel When ItГўВҖВҷs Correct

When the chain works:

- abs feel **very active**
- shoulders feel **supported**, not strained
- legs feel **lighter**
- toes start to **deweight naturally**

If shoulders feel like theyГўВҖВҷre dying, the core chain broke.

## Message 163

## ГўВңВ… What YouГўВҖВҷre Doing Well

The rings are not drifting away from your body. That keeps lat engagement high.

**4ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Core engagement**

## ГўВҡВ ГҜВёВҸ The One Limiting Factor I See

ГўВҖВў It shifts work to the arms  
ГўВҖВў It makes the tuck feel much heavier than it should

ГўВҖВў Your torso lengthens  
ГўВҖВў The tuck feels lighter

1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Dead hang  
2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ **Depress scapula (long neck)**  
3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ **Push rings down hard**  
4ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ THEN lift into tuck

If you skip step 2, the hold will always feel harder.

ГўВҖВў arms straight

## Message 168

Good ГўВҖВ” that detail is actually very informative.

**Arms shaking** in a tuck front lever usually does **not** mean your arms are the weak link. It almost always means your **scapular stabilizers and lats are reaching their endurance limit**, and the arms are compensating to keep the structure from collapsing.

From the frames you sent, the chain looks like this right now:

```
Core: good
Compression: good
Rings position: good
Scap depression: improving
Lat endurance: limiting
Arms: compensating ГўВҶВ’ shaking
```

So the shaking is basically your nervous system saying:

> ГўВҖВңHold the structure together!ГўВҖВқ

ThatГўВҖВҷs normal at your stage.

---

## The Mechanical Reason

When the **lats fatigue**, the system shifts load to:

- biceps  
- brachialis  
- elbow flexors  

Those muscles are **not designed for straight-arm lever work**, so they tremble.

The fix is **lat endurance and scapular stability**, not arm strength.

---

## The Quick Cue That Will Reduce Arm Shake

When you're in the tuck, think:

**ГўВҖВңPush the rings down toward my hips.ГўВҖВқ**

Not pull.

That cue:

- increases lat engagement  
- reduces elbow tension  
- stabilizes the scapula

You should feel more load move into your **mid-back and armpits**.

From hang:

2. hold 2 seconds  
3. relax  
4. repeat ГғВ—5

Then go immediately into your tuck hold.

This pre-activates the lats and reduces the arm shake.

- how to stabilize a straight-arm lever

ThatГўВҖВҷs the exact adaptation phase before front lever holds start to suddenly extend in duration.

That jump usually happens quickly once the scap endurance adapts.

Instead of:

```
pull ГўВҶВ’ elbows back ГўВҶВ’ chest over
```

YouГўВҖВҷre missing the **aggressive elbow whip**.

## The Magic Cue For Your Next Attempts

At the top of the pull think:

**ГўВҖВңELBOWS TO MY BACK POCKETS.ГўВҖВқ**

Not down.  
Not behind the bar.

**Behind your body.**

This rotates your shoulders around the bar.

## Message 179

That feeling is **exactly the right diagnosis**, Ryan. What youГўВҖВҷre describing is the **most common reason people stall right before their first muscle-up**.

Your elbows are doing this:

```
pull
   \   elbows flare out
    \
     stop
```

But a muscle-up requires this:

```
pull
   \
    \  elbows drive BACK
     \
      chest goes over bar
```

When the elbows flare **out to the sides**, your body enters a **wide pull-up pattern**. That locks your shoulders and **prevents the turnover**.

When the elbows go **back**, your shoulders rotate and your chest can come **over the bar**.

---

# The Fix (Very Simple Cue)

On the next rep think:

**ГўВҖВңCrack a walnut in my armpits.ГўВҖВқ**

or even simpler:

**ГўВҖВңElbows to ribs.ГўВҖВқ**

This keeps the elbows **tight and driving behind you** instead of flaring.

---

# Another Cue That Works REALLY Well

Instead of pulling the bar **down**, think:

**ГўВҖВңRow the bar to my belly button.ГўВҖВқ**

This automatically sends the elbows **behind you**.

YouГўВҖВҷll feel your **lats light up immediately**.

---

# One More Key Detail I Noticed

In your photos youГўВҖВҷre doing something **very correct** already:

YouГўВҖВҷre bringing your **feet forward**.

That is perfect.

But when the elbows flare, your body does this:

```
hips forward
chest stays back
```

When the elbows go back, your body does this:

```
hips forward
chest comes OVER bar
```

ThatГўВҖВҷs the missing piece.

---

# Tiny Drill (30 seconds that helps a ton)

Before your next attempt:

Do **5 slow pull-ups** with this cue:

**ГўВҖВңdrag elbows down my ribs.ГўВҖВқ**

Imagine your elbows sliding down the sides of your body.

Then do your explosive pull.

Your brain will automatically keep them tight.

---

# The Moment YouГўВҖВҷll Know It Worked

When the elbows go back correctly you will feel:

ГўВҖВў the bar suddenly feel **lower**  
ГўВҖВў your **sternum touches the bar**  
ГўВҖВў your body feels like it wants to **tip over**

That ГўВҖВңtippingГўВҖВқ feeling is the **turnover beginning**.

---

# Honest Feedback

YouГўВҖВҷre **one technical cue away** right now.

Your strength, hollow body, and pull height are already good enough.

This is the **coordination phase**.

And that usually unlocks **fast** once the cue clicks.

---

**Long neck ГўВҶВ’ hollow ГўВҶВ’ pull bar to belly ГўВҶВ’ elbows to ribs**

## Message 181

Ryan ГўВҖВ” this frame is **very close** to the moment where the first muscle-up happens. ThereГўВҖВҷs one specific mechanical thing happening here that explains why youГўВҖВҷre *almost* getting over but not quite.

---

## What You Did Really Well Here

### 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ The bar is at the **correct height**
The bar is basically at your **lower chest / upper stomach**.

That means your **pull strength is already sufficient** for a muscle-up. Many people stall because they can only reach chin height ГўВҖВ” youГўВҖВҷre well past that.

---

### 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Your feet are forward
Your body is doing the correct **muscle-up arc**:

```
hang
 ГўВҶВ’ hollow
 ГўВҶВ’ feet forward
 ГўВҶВ’ hips forward
 ГўВҶВ’ bar to chest
```

That arc is exactly what allows the body to rotate over the bar.

---

### 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Your shoulders are still depressed
You kept the **long neck / shoulders down** cue.

ThatГўВҖВҷs why your lats are doing the work instead of your arms.

---

# The One Thing Blocking the Turnover

Your **chest is still behind the bar**.

Even though you pulled high enough, your body position stayed like this:

```
bar
|
|   chest
|
```

Instead of:

```
chest
|
bar
|
```

That tiny shift is the **turnover moment**.

---

# Why ItГўВҖВҷs Happening

Your elbows are **still slightly flaring outward**.

That causes the pull to finish like a pull-up instead of rotating your torso.

Right now your arms are doing this:

```
\     /
 \   /
  \ /
```

They need to do this:

```
|   |
|   |
|   |
```

Then drive **behind you**.

---

# The Cue That Will Fix This

At the top of the pull think:

**ГўВҖВңLean over the bar.ГўВҖВқ**

Not *pull higher*.

Lean forward like youГўВҖВҷre trying to **look at the ground on the other side of the bar**.

Your chest should move **over the bar**, not just up to it.

---

# The Trick That Helps People Instantly

Right when the bar reaches your chest:

**Throw your head and chest forward.**

It feels weird because instinct says pull up.

But muscle-ups require this:

```
UP ГўВҶВ’ FORWARD ГўВҶВ’ PRESS
```

Not just up.

---

# Something Very Encouraging

Your **legs are doing the correct thing now**.

Earlier in the session they were lifting like a knee raise.

Now they are acting like a **counterweight**, which is exactly what high-level athletes do.

ThatГўВҖВҷs why youГўВҖВҷre suddenly getting so close.

---

# Your Progression Right Now

Honestly this is where you are:

```
strength ГўВңВ”
pull height ГўВңВ”
hollow body ГўВңВ”
bar path ГўВңВ”
turnover timing ГўВҸВі
```

Which is the **final stage before the first rep**.

## Message 183

That insight is **exactly right**, Ryan. What you're feeling is the nervous system issue almost everyone hits before their first muscle-up.

Your brain has thousands of reps of this pattern:

```
pull-up
UP ГўВҶВ’ STOP ГўВҶВ’ DOWN
```

But a muscle-up is a **completely different motor pattern**:

```
UP ГўВҶВ’ FORWARD ГўВҶВ’ PRESS
```

Your strength is already enough ГўВҖВ” your nervous system just hasn't wired the **pull ГўВҶВ’ push transition** yet.

The good news: that phase usually resolves **very quickly** once you practice the right pattern.

---

# The Key Concept

Think of a muscle-up as:

**an explosive row followed immediately by a dip**

Not a high pull-up.

```
ROW ГўВҶВ’ CHEST OVER ГўВҶВ’ DIP
```

That mental model helps a lot.

---

Instead of thinking **pull up**, think:

**ГўВҖВңPull the bar to my hips.ГўВҖВқ**

This forces the correct arc.

Imagine there is a window above the bar and you're pushing your **head and chest through it**.

That automatically starts the turnover.

Your body currently stops here:

```
         |
bar ------------
```

But the muscle-up requires this shift:

```

   |
   |
bar ----------
```

Your chest must **pass over the bar**, not just reach it.

## Why Your Surfing Felt Better

1. **Reactive balance**

- knee tracking

On a surfboard that translates to:

## Message 191

ThatГўВҖВҷs actually **very normal**, and the fact that youГўВҖВҷre noticing the **butt wink** and where the stretch moves is a sign your body awareness is improving. The important thing is *why* itГўВҖВҷs happening and how to refine it without fighting your body.

---

## Г°ВҹВ§В  What the ГўВҖВңButt WinkГўВҖВқ Really Is
A butt wink is simply **posterior pelvic tilt at the bottom of a squat**. In a pistol, it happens when your body runs out of hip flexion range and the pelvis rotates to continue descending.

Mechanically it looks like:

```
hips reach limit
ГўВҶВ“
pelvis tucks under
ГўВҶВ“
lumbar spine rounds slightly
```

In **deep single-leg squats**, a small amount of this is **completely normal**. Elite athletes often have a little wink in pistols because the range is extreme.

The key question isnГўВҖВҷt ГўВҖВңdoes it exist?ГўВҖВқ but **when it happens and whether you control it**.

---

## Г°ВҹВ‘ВҚ The Good Sign in Your Case
You said you feel the stretch in **hips and glutes**, not your lower back.

That means the load is being absorbed mostly by:

- glutes
- hip capsule
- deep hip flexion

Not the lumbar spine.

ThatГўВҖВҷs exactly what we want.

---

## Why Your Body Is Doing This
Three things typically contribute:

1. **Hip flexion limit**
   Your femur reaches its flexion limit relative to the pelvis.

2. **Pelvis orientation**
   Your pelvis rotates to allow deeper range.

3. **Ankle mobility**
   Limited dorsiflexion can push the pelvis to compensate.

The good news: you already said your **dorsiflexion and ankle function are improving**, so one of the big contributors is already resolving.

---

## Г°ВҹВ”В§ The Small Adjustment That Helps Most
Instead of thinking ГўВҖВңstay straight,ГўВҖВқ think:

> **ГўВҖВңStay tall until the last inch.ГўВҖВқ**

Meaning:

- maintain your brace
- control descent
- let the pelvis rotate **only at the very bottom**

This prevents the wink from happening early.

---

## Г°ВҹВҰВө Two Simple Drills That Help Pistols

### 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Counterbalance Pistols
Hold a small plate or object in front of you.

This lets your torso stay more upright, reducing early pelvic tuck.

### 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Deep Squat Hold (Assisted)
Hold a post or rings and sit in the bottom position for 20ГўВҖВ“30 seconds.

Focus on:

```
knees forward
chest tall
hips relaxed
```

This gradually increases comfortable hip flexion.

---

## Г°ВҹВҢВҠ Why You Feel It in the Hips/Glutes
ThatГўВҖВҷs actually a **positive adaptation**.

It means:

- your glutes are lengthening under load
- hip capsule mobility is improving
- posterior chain tension is redistributing

Many people with ГўВҖВңtight hamstringsГўВҖВқ discover that once hips start moving properly, the tightness shifts there temporarily.

---

## Г°ВҹВҡВҰ What to Watch For
Your butt wink is fine if:

- it happens **only near the bottom**
- thereГўВҖВҷs **no lower-back pain**
- you maintain tension and control

If it starts early or causes discomfort, then weГўВҖВҷd adjust range or stance.

---

# Why Ankles Are the Secret

Your ankle is the **first shock absorber** in the system.

If the ankle canГўВҖВҷt control force:

```
force travels upward
ГўВҶВ’ knee collapses
ГўВҶВ’ hip compensates
ГўВҶВ’ balance is lost
```

Pistols train the ankle to **control force instead of just receiving it**.

ThatГўВҖВҷs the difference between:

```
stiff landing
vs

```

What youГўВҖВҷre describingГўВҖВ”being able to ГўВҖВңgrab the groundГўВҖВқГўВҖВ”is the intrinsic foot muscles turning on and coordinating with the ankle and hip. - **Big toe mound**
- **Little toe mound**

- **Flexor hallucis brevis**
- **Lumbricals**

```

ГўВҶВ“

ГўВҶВ“
knee tracks correctly
ГўВҶВ“
hip stabilizes
ГўВҶВ“

```

Most peopleГўВҖВҷs feet are passive from years of shoes and flat surfaces. When they start working again, the body suddenly has **much richer balance feedback**. ThatГўВҖВҷs why sports like surfing, skating, or trail running feel easierГўВҖВ”youГўВҖВҷre getting real-time micro-adjustments from the ground.

# How to Grow Your Biceps (Without Ruining Your Skill Work)

There are **three levers** for bicep growth:

1. **Enough volume**
2. **Full stretch**
3. **Controlled tempo**

You can add these without interfering with your pull training.

---

# The 3 Best Exercises For You

Since you already use rings and bars, these fit perfectly.

## 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Ring Bicep Curls (Top Recommendation)

These are fantastic for calisthenics athletes.

Setup:
- rings shoulder height
- lean back
- palms facing you
- curl body toward rings

3ГўВҖВ“4 sets ГғВ— 8ГўВҖВ“12 reps

Focus on:
```
elbows stay high
full extension
slow lowering
```

This gives a **deep stretch**, which is huge for growth.

---

## 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Chin-Ups (Underhand Pull-Ups)

These load the biceps heavily.

3ГўВҖВ“4 sets ГғВ— 5ГўВҖВ“8 reps

Cue:
```
pull elbows to ribs
bar to chest
slow descent
```

These build **thickness**.

---

## 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Dumbbell or Band Curls

Classic but effective.

3 sets ГғВ— 10ГўВҖВ“15 reps.

Use slow tempo:

```
2 sec up
3 sec down
```

The slow negative stimulates growth.

---

# Weekly Volume Target

For visible growth:

**10ГўВҖВ“16 total bicep sets per week**

YouГўВҖВҷre probably already getting ~6ГўВҖВ“8 from pull workouts.

Add **4ГўВҖВ“6 direct sets**.

ThatГўВҖВҷs enough.

# Example Integration With Your Current Plan

**Day 2 (Pull Day)**

After your muscle-up work:

ГўВҖВў Ring curls ГўВҖВ“ 3 ГғВ— 10  
ГўВҖВў Chin-ups ГўВҖВ“ 3 ГғВ— 6

# One Trick That Works Extremely Well

At the bottom of curls:

This loads the bicep in its lengthened position.

ThatГўВҖВҷs where the **most growth stimulus happens**.

# Nutrition Matters Too

You mentioned earlier you might not be eating enough.

For muscle growth aim for:

**0.7ГўВҖВ“1g protein per lb bodyweight**

At ~190 lb thatГўВҖВҷs roughly:

**130ГўВҖВ“170g protein per day**

Without enough protein, the arms wonГўВҖВҷt grow much even if training is perfect.

---

# Realistic Timeline

If you train consistently and eat enough:

You should start noticing:

- fuller biceps in **4ГўВҖВ“6 weeks**
- visible size difference in **8ГўВҖВ“12 weeks**

Especially because your pull strength is already improving.

---

# One Important Detail

If your goal is **aesthetic arm size**, the exercise most calisthenics athletes miss is:

**ring curls**

They give the best stimulus for biceps with bodyweight.

If you want, I can also show you **a 5-minute ГўВҖВңarm finisherГўВҖВқ** that calisthenics athletes use to add bicep size without hurting pull performance.

## Message 198

Great question ГўВҖВ” and perfect timing to ask it.

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  Why Plyos Make Sense *for you right now*

YouГўВҖВҷve built:
- **control** (pistols, shrimp squats)  
- **mobility** (dorsiflexion improving)  
- **stability** (foot tripod, ankle control)

Plyos add:
- **reactivity**
- **elastic return**
- **sport transfer (surfing, etc.)**

So the progression becomes:

```text
control ГўВҶВ’ strength ГўВҶВ’ elasticity
```

YouГўВҖВҷre ready for step 3 in small doses.

---

# ГўВҡВ ГҜВёВҸ The Rule (Important)

Plyos should feel:

ГўВңВ” springy  
ГўВңВ” light  
ГўВңВ” crisp  

NOT:
ГўВқВҢ grinding  
ГўВқВҢ heavy  
ГўВқВҢ fatiguing  

If it feels like work ГўВҶВ’ you went too far.

---

# Г°ВҹВҰВө DAY 3 ГўВҖВ” Legs + Smart Plyometrics

## 0ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Prep (3ГўВҖВ“4 min)

Wake up the ankle.

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ BLOCK 1 ГўВҖВ” Plyometric Primer (NEW)

### 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Pogo Jumps ГўВҖВ” 3ГғВ—20
Feet together, minimal knee bend.

Cue:
```text
bounce through ankles
stay tall
quick contacts
```

This builds your **ankle spring**.

---

### 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Split Stance Switch Jumps ГўВҖВ” 3ГғВ—5/side

Start in a lunge ГўВҶВ’ lightly switch in air.

- soft landing  
- balance on landing  

This translates directly to pistols + surfing.

ГўВҖВў 3ГғВ—4 assisted  
ГўВҖВў optional slow negative

# Г°ВҹВ”Вө BLOCK 3 ГўВҖВ” Shrimp Squats (Progression)

### 4ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Shrimp Squats ГўВҖВ” 3ГғВ—5

Now add:
- **3 sec down**
- **1 sec pause at bottom**

You said these feel strong ГўВҖВ” now we deepen control.

---

# Г°ВҹВҹВЈ BLOCK 4 ГўВҖВ” Stability + Power Blend

### 5ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Reverse Lunge ГўВҶВ’ Knee Drive Hop ГўВҖВ” 3ГғВ—5/side

- plyo (hop)

Stick the landing each rep.

---

# Г°ВҹВҹВў BLOCK 5 ГўВҖВ” Core

Choose:

# Г°ВҹВҡВҖ Optional Finisher (Only if feeling great)

Your shoulders are doing a lot of the work.

```text

```

> **ГўВҖВңpush the floor forwardГўВҖВқ**

That increases protraction and takes pressure off the shoulders.

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү Loss of elbow lock + wrist load =

# Г°ВҹВ§В  What Just Happened (Important)

When you used the **ГўВҖВңfall forwardГўВҖВқ cue**, your body did:

```text

ГўВҶВ“

ГўВҶВ“

ГўВҶВ“

```

So:
- **shoulders = strong enough**
- **core = engaging**
- ГўВқВ— **straight-arm + wrist tolerance = limiting factor**

ThatГўВҖВҷs a *very normal progression point*.

---

# ГўВҡВ ГҜВёВҸ Why You Felt It In Your Wrist

When elbows unlock slightly:

```text

shoulders ГўВҶВ’ elbows ГўВҶВ’ wrists
```

Instead of stacking force through the arm, you end up **hinging at the wrist**.

ThatГўВҖВҷs why it felt sharp/noticeable.

- triceps
- connective tissue tension

> ГўВҖВңI can grab the groundГўВҖВқ

As you lean:

```text
fingers press down
ГўВҶВ“

ГўВҶВ“
takes pressure off wrist joint
```

Cue:

> **ГўВҖВңclaw the ground as I fallГўВҖВқ**

## Message 222

Great question ГўВҖВ” this is one of the **most important concepts** for everything youГўВҖВҷre doing (planche, muscle-ups, HSPU, even surfing).

LetГўВҖВҷs make it super clear and tied to what you *feel*.

---

# Г°ВҹВҰВҙ Scapula Basics (Shoulder Blades)

Your shoulder blades can move in different directions on your ribcage.

The two youГўВҖВҷre asking about:

---

# ГўВһВЎГҜВёВҸ **Protraction (Push Forward)**

Г®ВҲВҖimage_groupГ®ВҲВӮ{"aspect_ratio":"1:1","query":["scapular protraction diagram push up shoulder blades spread","rounded upper back push up protraction position","planche scapula protraction position","serratus anterior activation protraction"],"num_per_query":1}Г®ВҲВҒ

### What it is:
Shoulder blades move **away from your spine**

Think:
```text
ГўВҖВңpush the ground awayГўВҖВқ
ГўВҖВңspread your upper backГўВҖВқ
```

### What it feels like:
- upper back rounds slightly  
- chest moves away from floor  
- you feel **serratus (side ribs/under armpit)**  

### Where you use it:
- planche ГўВңВ… (huge)
- push-ups (top position)
- surfing pop-up (this is what you felt)
- plank / hollow positions

---

# ГўВ¬ВҮГҜВёВҸ **Depression (Pull Down)**

Г®ВҲВҖimage_groupГ®ВҲВӮ{"aspect_ratio":"1:1","query":["scapular depression pull up shoulders down position lats engaged","dead hang active shoulders depression","gymnastic rings support hold depression shoulders down","lat activation shoulders down and back"],"num_per_query":1}Г®ВҲВҒ

### What it is:
Shoulders move **down away from your ears**

Think:
```text
ГўВҖВңlong neckГўВҖВқ
ГўВҖВңshoulders in back pocketsГўВҖВқ
```

### What it feels like:
- lats engage  
- traps relax (no shrugging)  
- chest feels more open  

### Where you use it:
- pull-ups / muscle-ups ГўВңВ…
- dead hangs (active)
- front lever
- ring support

---

# ГўВҡВЎ The Key Insight (This is where youГўВҖВҷre leveling up)

These are NOT opposites.

You often use them **together**.

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ Example: Planche (what youГўВҖВҷve been feeling)

YouГўВҖВҷre doing:

```text
protraction + depression
```

Meaning:
- push the ground away (protraction)
- keep shoulders down (depression)

That creates:
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү insane stability  
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү that ГўВҖВңconnectedГўВҖВқ feeling you described  

---

# Г°ВҹВҢВҠ Example: Surf Pop-Up (what you just experienced)

You did this without realizing:

- hands hit board ГўВҶВ’ **protraction (push)**
- shoulders stayed strong ГўВҶВ’ **depression (no collapse)**

ThatГўВҖВҷs why:
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү you didnГўВҖВҷt sink  
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү you could redirect into the face  

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  Quick Cheat Sheet

```text
PROTRACTION = push / spread
DEPRESSION  = down / anchor
```

---

# Г°ВҹВ§Вӯ Why This Matters For You

Right now your breakthroughs are coming from:

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү learning how to **position your scapula**, not just move your arms  

ThatГўВҖВҷs why:
- your muscle-up is clicking

- your HSPU is right there


# Г°ВҹВҢВҠ WhatГўВҖВҷs Actually Happening in Your Pop-Up

### Spine:
- extends slightly (your ГўВҖВңscorpionГўВҖВқ feel)

```text
stable shoulders + free spine = smooth pop-up
```


YouГўВҖВҷre doing neither.

## Message 241

Great question ГўВҖВ” and this is a **huge unlock** for your core, front lever, and even muscle-up control.

Short answer:

> **You hinge at the hips ГўВҖВ” but initiate from the pelvis (posterior tilt).**

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  What Most People Do (Incorrect)

They do:

```text
legs lift
ГўВҶВ’ hips stay neutral
ГўВҶВ’ lower abs disengaged
```

That turns it into:
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү hip flexor exercise  
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү swinging legs  
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү weak core carryover  

---

# Г°ВҹВ”В‘ What YOU Want (Correct Pattern)

You want:

```text
posterior pelvic tilt
ГўВҶВ’ THEN hips flex
ГўВҶВ’ knees rise
```

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ The Key Cue (this will click for you)

> **ГўВҖВңtuck my tailbone, then lift my kneesГўВҖВқ**

---

# ГўВҡВҷГҜВёВҸ Step-by-Step Breakdown

From a hang:

### 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Set the base
- **depress shoulders** (long neck)  
- slight hollow  

---

### 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Initiate with pelvis
Before knees move:

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү **tilt pelvis back**

Think:
```text
belt buckle ГўВҶВ’ toward ribs
```

---

### 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Then lift knees
Now:

- knees come up  
- hips fold  

But the movement started from:
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү core, not legs  

---

# Г°ВҹВ§ВӘ Quick Test (youГўВҖВҷll feel this immediately)

Try 2 reps:

### Rep A (wrong)
- just lift knees  

### Rep B (correct)
- tuck pelvis first  
- THEN lift  

YouГўВҖВҷll feel:

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү way more lower abs  
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү less swinging  
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү more control  

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  Why This Matters for YOU

This directly connects to:

### Front lever
```text
hips up = same pelvic control
```

### Planche
```text
ГўВҖВңshorten the frontГўВҖВқ = same tilt
```

### Muscle-up
```text
body stays connected during pull
```

---

# ГўВҡВЎ Advanced Cue (since you're progressing fast)

Instead of thinking knees up:

> **ГўВҖВңlift my hips toward my ribsГўВҖВқ**

Knees just follow.

---

# Г°ВҹВ§Вӯ What It Should Feel Like

ГўВңВ” abs engage first  
ГўВңВ” movement is slower + tighter  
ГўВңВ” no swing  
ГўВңВ” top feels like compression  

Not:
ГўВқВҢ leg lift  
ГўВқВҢ momentum  
ГўВқВҢ hip flexor burn only  

---

# Г°ВҹВ’ВҘ One Line to Remember

If everything else disappears:

> **ГўВҖВңpelvis moves first, knees follow.ГўВҖВқ**

## Message 248

How can I warm up my elbows and protect them I feel a tightness where my triceps connects to the elbow

---

## Message 249

Good catch ГўВҖВ” that exact spot (tricep tendon at the elbow) is **where a lot of calisthenics guys get irritated** when pushing volume + leans + dips.

The fact you *feel it early* = we can fix it before it becomes a problem.

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  What YouГўВҖВҷre Feeling

That tightness is usually:

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү **triceps tendon + connective tissue load**  
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү from:
- planche leans (elbow lock + forward load)  
- dips (deep elbow flexion)  
- push-ups (repetition)  

---

# Г°ВҹВ”В‘ Goal

Not just ГўВҖВңstretch itГўВҖВқ ГўВҖВ” we want:

```text
heat ГўВҶВ’ blood flow ГўВҶВ’ controlled load ГўВҶВ’ joint readiness
```

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ Your Elbow Warmup (5 min ГўВҖВ” do this EVERY push day)

## Г°ВҹВҹВЎ 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Tissue Warmup (1ГўВҖВ“2 min)

### Tricep Massage (quick)
- use thumb or fingers  
- rub above elbow (back of arm)

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү 30ГўВҖВ“60s each side  

Goal:
> wake up the tendon, not smash it

---

## Г°ВҹВ”Вө 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Active Range (no load yet)

### Arm Circles ГўВҖВ” 10 each direction  
### Elbow Flex + Extend ГўВҖВ” 15 reps  

Then:

### Tricep Stretch (light)
- overhead arm  
- gentle pull  

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү donГўВҖВҷt force it

---

## Г°ВҹВҹВЈ 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Tendon Prep (MOST IMPORTANT)

### Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ Straight Arm Lean (very light) ГўВҖВ” 2ГғВ—15ГўВҖВ“20s

- hands on floor  
- elbows locked  
- slight forward lean  

Cue:
```text
lock ГўВҶВ’ rotate elbows forward ГўВҶВ’ gentle pressure
```

This:
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү preloads tendon safely  
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү tells your body ГўВҖВңweГўВҖВҷre about to use thisГўВҖВқ

---

## Г°ВҹВҹВў 4ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Activation (prime the system)

### Scap Push-Ups ГўВҖВ” 2ГғВ—10  
### Incline Push-Ups ГўВҖВ” 1ГғВ—10 (easy)

Focus:
- smooth reps  
- no strain  

---

# ГўВҡВ ГҜВёВҸ Key Protection Rules (for YOU specifically)

## 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ DonГўВҖВҷt slam into straight-arm load cold
Planche lean = high tendon stress

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү always ramp into it

---

## 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Micro-bend is OK early

At the start of your session:
- donГўВҖВҷt force aggressive lockout immediately  
- let tendon warm up  

---

## 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Watch deep dips

If you feel that spot:

Г°ВҹВ‘Вү reduce depth slightly  
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү keep shoulders engaged (no sinking)

---

# Г°ВҹВ’ВЎ Quick Self-Test

- slight bend

```text
tells tendon = we are safe
```

ГўВҶВ’ just do slow air extensions

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ Why It Feels Confusing

Because when things start clicking, they often happen **at the same time**.

So it feels like:
> ГўВҖВңIs this depression? Is this protraction?ГўВҖВқ

Answer:
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү itГўВҖВҷs usually **both layered together**

---

# Г°ВҹВҹВЎ What YouГўВҖВҷre Feeling Right Now

When you said:

YouГўВҖВҷre probably feeling a mix of:

### Depression
- shoulders down  
- lats engaged  
- ГўВҖВңstable baseГўВҖВқ

AND

### Protraction
- pushing the ground away

- serratus firing

# Г°ВҹВ”Вө How to Tell Them Apart (easy test)

## Try this:

### 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Shrug up (ears to shoulders)
ГўВҶВ’ opposite of depression

### 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Pull shoulders down (long neck)
ГўВҶВ’ **depression**

---

### Now:

### 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Push your hands into the wall
ГўВҶВ’ upper back spreads  
ГўВҶВ’ **protraction**

---

# ГўВҡВЎ What You Use Where (for YOU)

## Planche / Push Work
```text
protraction + depression
```

- push forward  
- keep shoulders down  

---

## Pull-ups / Muscle-ups
```text

then slight protraction during transition
```

---

## Front Lever
```text

minimal protraction
```

# Г°ВҹВҰВ¶ What ГўВҖВңShort FootГўВҖВқ Means (quick reset)


# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ DAY 2 ГўВҖВ” PULL / MUSCLE-UP / COMPRESSION

# Г°ВҹВ§ВҳГўВҖВҚГўВҷВӮГҜВёВҸ 0ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Breath + Intent (2ГўВҖВ“3 min)

## Г°ВҹВҢВ¬ГҜВёВҸ Breathing

- inhale through nose

## Г°ВҹВҺВІ Mindful Reminder
> **ГўВҖВңStrength without awareness becomes tension.ГўВҖВқ**

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҒ Warmup Flow (6 min)

## Г°ВҹВҹВЎ Scap + Elbow Prep
### 2 rounds:
- scap pullups x8
- active dead hang x20s
- slow elbow flex/extend x10
- wrist circles x10 each

Focus:
```text id="wddxbo"
smooth depression
smooth elevation
```

---

## Г°ВҹВ”Вө Compression Prep
### Seated compression lifts
- 2ГғВ—10

Then:
### Hanging tuck hold
- 2ГғВ—15s

Cue:
> **ГўВҖВңCompress first.ГўВҖВқ**

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ BLOCK 1 ГўВҖВ” Scap Pullups

## 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Scap Pullups ГўВҖВ” 4ГғВ—5

Do NOT bend elbows.

Movement:
```text id="6a2gkz"
depress
slight retract
rise
```

Pause at top.

---

### Focus
Especially left side:
- smooth depression
- even shoulder motion

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ BLOCK 2 ГўВҖВ” Chest-to-Bar Pulls

## 2ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ High Pullups / Chest-to-Bar Attempts ГўВҖВ” 5ГғВ—3

Not max reps.

Explosive + controlled.

---

### Sequence
Think:
```text id="1sgx44"
compress
lean back slightly
drive elbows BACK
```

NOT:
```text id="o4hxmo"
chin up to survive
```

---

### Г°ВҹВ”В‘ Cue
> **ГўВҖВңPull bar to ribs.ГўВҖВқ**

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ BLOCK 3 ГўВҖВ” Muscle-Up Transition Drill

## 3ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Jumping Transition OR Negative Transition ГўВҖВ” 4ГғВ—3

Goal:
teach turnover mechanics safely.

---

### Focus
- elbows rotate OVER
- chest stays close
- hollow stays connected

---

### IMPORTANT
Do NOT grind ugly reps.

WeГўВҖВҷre wiring mechanics.

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ BLOCK 4 ГўВҖВ” Hanging Compression

## 4ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Hanging Knee Raises ГўВҖВ” 3ГғВ—8

But now:
### compress BEFORE movement

Sequence:
```text id="b6mtbq"
posterior tilt
ribs down
knees rise
```

---

## Optional Advanced Rep
At top:
- tiny pause
- try to ГўВҖВңfoldГўВҖВқ

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ BLOCK 5 ГўВҖВ” Tuck Front Lever Awareness

## 5ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Tuck Lever Holds ГўВҖВ” 3ГғВ—10ГўВҖВ“15s

Small tuck.

No ego.

---

- depress scap
- hollow
- hips tucked

This is huge for:
- lats

- surf paddle structure

---

# Г°ВҹВҹВў BLOCK 6 ГўВҖВ” Bicep Density

## 6ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Chin-Ups OR Ring Chin-Ups ГўВҖВ” 3ГғВ—5 slow

3-second lower.

---

### Cue
> **ГўВҖВңStretch then pull.ГўВҖВқ**

This is your bicep growth goldmine.

---

# Г°ВҹВ§ВҠ Optional Finisher

## Dead Hang ГўВҖВ” 1ГўВҖВ“2 min accumulated

Relax grip slightly.

Let shoulders breathe.

Because your left side likely:
- struggles to stabilize scapula

# Г°ВҹВ”В‘ Important Nuance

This does NOT mean:
> ГўВҖВңalways max protract everythingГўВҖВқ

It means:
```text id="a58bxt"
use enough protraction to create support
```

The right amount depends on the movement.

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В© In Face Pulls / Ring Chinups

What youГўВҖВҷre discovering is:

### BAD pattern
```text id="r0hr2w"
arm pulls first
```

### BETTER pattern
```text id="fskjlwm"
scap positions
then arm expresses force
```

ThatГўВҖВҷs the athletic pattern.

---

# Г°ВҹВҢВҠ This Also Explains Your Surf Insight

Remember when you said:
- depression creates the base
- then protraction lets you pop up?

This is the SAME concept.

Your body likes:
```text id="p6phw8"
stable scap ГўВҶВ’ efficient force transfer
```

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ The Big Upgrade

YouГўВҖВҷre beginning to understand:
> scap position changes EVERYTHING downstream

ThatГўВҖВҷs advanced movement awareness.

Because youГўВҖВҷre finally sharing load correctly.

## Message 288

Excellent question ГўВҖВ” and this is where movement training and bodybuilding overlap but arenГўВҖВҷt identical.

The answer is:

> **Sometimes yes, sometimes no ГўВҖВ” depends what youГўВҖВҷre trying to bias.**

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В  First: Why Protraction Helped You

In your ring chin / face pull work:

Protraction helped because it:
- stabilized your scap
- reduced compensation
- let force transfer better

So for **healthy mechanics**, some protraction (or controlled scap positioning) was absolutely the right move.

---

# Г°ВҹВ’ВӘ But For Pure Bicep Growth?

The goal shifts slightly.

For biceps, you generally want:
```text id="2pym1x"
stable scap
+
elbow flexion under stretch
```

NOT:
```text id="r6x4zm"
maximal protraction all the time
```

Because too much protraction can:
- reduce lat contribution weirdly
- alter line of pull
- turn it into more serratus/upper-back work

---

# Г°ВҹВ”В‘ The Sweet Spot For YOU

You likely need:
```text id="d8p79r"
ENOUGH protraction for shoulder stability
but not excessive protraction
```

Think:
- stable shoulder blade
- relaxed neck
- clean elbow path

Then:
Г°ВҹВ‘Вү let the bicep actually load.

---

# Г°ВҹВ”ВҘ What This Means In Practice

## Г°ВҹВҹВЎ Ring Chin-Ups (best for you right now)

### Bottom:
- slight protraction/reach is OK
- scap free to move naturally

### Pull:
- depress + stabilize
- elbows drive down/front

### Top:
- chest tall
- donГўВҖВҷt aggressively round

---

# ГўВҡВЎ What You DONГўВҖВҷT Want

ГўВқВҢ shrugging  
ГўВқВҢ anterior shoulder dump  
ГўВқВҢ bicep tendon stabilizing shoulder  

ThatГўВҖВҷs what protraction was helping you avoid.

---

# Г°ВҹВ§В© For Actual Bicep Hypertrophy

The BIGGEST things are:
```text id="o1s0jo"
stretch
control
supination
```

Not just scap position.

---

## 1ГҜВёВҸГўВғВЈ Ring Chin-Ups

- deep stretch

3ГўВҖВ“5 sec lower.

Later on.

Crazy forearm + bicep carryover.

# Г°ВҹВ§В  The Key Concept

Scap position should:
> SUPPORT the movement

not become the movement itself.
